        <div style="position:relative;width:26px;height:26px;border-radius:50%;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#F97316,#EA580C);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:11px;font-weight:800;color:#FFFFFF;overflow:hidden;">{{ userInitial }}<div style="{{ homeAvatarImgStyle }}"></div></div>
        <span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:600;margin-top:4px;">Perfil</span>
      </div>
    </div>

  </div>

</div>

<script type="text/x-dc" data-dc-script="">
const BUILD_ID = '__BUILD_ID__';
const SUPABASE_URL = 'https://mopyslyhjtnmvlksusjr.supabase.co';
const SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = 'sb_publishable_FAg_UJOAOLwMJCcMBhdj1w_cX37utvu';
let _supabaseClient = null;
function getSupabase() {
  if (!_supabaseClient) {
    if (!window.supabase) throw new Error('supabase-js aún no cargó');
    _supabaseClient = window.supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_ANON_KEY);
  }
  return _supabaseClient;
}
function waitForSupabase() {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    if (window.supabase) return resolve();
    const id = setInterval(() => {
      if (window.supabase) { clearInterval(id); resolve(); }
    }, 50);
  });
}

  // Shown only until real coaches exist in Supabase (profiles.role = 'coach').
  static MOCK_COACHES = [
    { id: 'mock-juan', real: false, name: 'Juan Pérez', price: '$450/mes', bio: 'Fuerza · Hipertrofia · 6 años de experiencia', hours: 'Disponible Lun–Vie, 6am–12pm' },
    { id: 'mock-maria', real: false, name: 'María López', price: '$500/mes', bio: 'Pérdida de grasa · HIIT · 4 años de experiencia', hours: 'Disponible Lun–Sáb, 4pm–9pm' },
    { id: 'mock-carlos', real: false, name: 'Carlos Ruiz', price: '$600/mes', bio: 'Rendimiento atlético · Movilidad · 8 años de experiencia', hours: 'Disponible Mar–Dom, 7am–2pm' },
  ];

  async fetchCoaches() {
    // La tabla profiles solo deja leer tu propia fila (RLS), así que el
    // directorio público de entrenadores vive en coach_profiles. El nombre y
    // la foto viajan dentro de certifications como __name:/__avatar:.
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data, error } = await getSupabase().from('coach_profiles').select('*');
    if (error || !data) { this.setState({ coaches: [] }); return; }
    const real = data.map(cp => {
      const certs = Array.isArray(cp.certifications) ? cp.certifications : [];
      const nameTag = certs.find(c => typeof c === 'string' && c.indexOf('__name:') === 0);
      const avatarTag = certs.find(c => typeof c === 'string' && c.indexOf('__avatar:') === 0);
      return {
        id: cp.profile_id,
        real: true,
        name: nameTag ? nameTag.slice(7) : 'Entrenador',
        avatar: avatarTag && avatarTag.length > 9 ? avatarTag.slice(9) : null,
        price: (() => {
          if (!cp.monthly_price) return 'Precio a convenir';
          const pt = certs.find(c => typeof c === 'string' && c.indexOf('__period:') === 0);
          const per = pt ? pt.slice(9) : 'mes';
          return '$' + cp.monthly_price + '/' + per;
        })(),
        bio: cp.bio || 'Entrenador certificado',
        hours: cp.available_hours || '',
      };
    });
    // filtra por la sucursal elegida por el miembro (staff_branches es lectura pública)
    let visibles = real;
    try {
      const myBranch = this.state.memberBranchId;
      if (myBranch) {
        const { data: sbr } = await getSupabase().from('staff_branches').select('staff_id, branch_id');
        if (sbr && sbr.length) {
          const byCoach = {};
          sbr.forEach(x => { (byCoach[x.staff_id] = byCoach[x.staff_id] || []).push(x.branch_id); });
          visibles = real.filter(c => !byCoach[c.id] || byCoach[c.id].indexOf(myBranch) !== -1);
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {}
    this.setState({ coaches: visibles });
  }

  async fetchBranches() {
    try {
      await waitForSupabase();
      const { data } = await getSupabase().from('branches').select('id, name').order('name');
      if (data && data.length) this.setState({ branchesList: data });
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  async setMemberBranch(id) {
    if (!this.state.session || !id) return;
    this.setState({ memberBranchId: id });
    await waitForSupabase();
    await getSupabase().from('member_profiles').upsert({ profile_id: this.state.session.user.id, branch_id: id }, { onConflict: 'profile_id' });
    this.fetchCoaches(); // los coaches del paso 5 se filtran por esta sucursal
  }

  async cycleMemberBranch() {
    let list = this.state.branchesList || [];
    if (!list.length) { await this.fetchBranches(); list = this.state.branchesList || []; }
    if (!list.length || !this.state.session) return;
    const idx = list.findIndex(b => b.id === this.state.memberBranchId);
    const next = list[(idx + 1) % list.length];
    this.setState({ memberBranchId: next.id });
    await waitForSupabase();
    await getSupabase().from('member_profiles').upsert({ profile_id: this.state.session.user.id, branch_id: next.id }, { onConflict: 'profile_id' });
    this.fetchCoaches();
  }

  async fetchPrograms() {
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data, error } = await getSupabase()
      .from('programs')
      .select('id, slug, title, level, duration_weeks, program_exercises(id, order_index, name, sets, reps, notes)')
      .not('slug', 'is', null);
    if (error || !data || !data.length) return; // keep MOCK_PROGRAMS fallback
    const bySlug = {};
    data.forEach(p => {
      const exercises = (p.program_exercises || []).slice().sort((a, b) => a.order_index - b.order_index);
      bySlug[p.slug] = {
        id: p.id,
        name: p.title,
        level: p.level || 'Intermedio',
        duration: String(Math.min(90, Math.max(20, Math.round(exercises.length * 4 / 5) * 5))),
        exercises: String(exercises.length),
        exerciseList: exercises.map(e => ({ id: e.id, name: e.name, subtitle: e.notes || '', setsReps: e.reps ? `${e.sets || '3'} × ${e.reps}` : (e.sets ? `${e.sets} series` : '3 × 12') })),
      };
    });
    if (Object.keys(bySlug).length) this.setState(s => ({ realPrograms: { ...s.realPrograms, ...bySlug } }));
  }

  async openCategoryPanel(key, name) {
    this.setState({ categoryPanelOpen: true, activeCategoryKey: key, activeCategoryName: name, categoryExercises: [], categoryLoading: true });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('exercise_catalog')
      .select('id, name, muscle_groups, equipment')
      .eq('category', key)
      .order('name');
    this.setState({ categoryExercises: data || [], categoryLoading: false });
  }

  async fetchAssignedProgram() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    const userId = this.state.session.user.id;
    const toEntry = (p) => {
      if (!p) return null;
      const exercises = (p.program_exercises || []).slice()
        .sort((a, b) => a.order_index - b.order_index)
        .map(e => ({ id: e.id, name: e.name, subtitle: e.notes || '', setsReps: e.reps ? `${e.sets || '3'} × ${e.reps}` : (e.sets ? `${e.sets} series` : '3 × 12') }));
      const estMins = Math.min(90, Math.max(20, Math.round(exercises.length * 4 / 5) * 5));
      let _tdays = [];
      try { _tdays = Array.isArray(p.training_days) ? p.training_days : JSON.parse(p.training_days || '[]'); } catch (_) { _tdays = []; }
      return { id: p.id, name: p.title, subtitle: `${p.title} · Activo`, level: p.level || 'Intermedio', category: 'PERSONALIZADO', duration: String(estMins), exercises: String(exercises.length), exerciseList: exercises, cover_image_url: p.cover_image_url || null, training_days: _tdays };
    };
    // 1) Coach-assigned programs — con retry si la columna training_days no existe
    let assignedRes = await sb.from('program_assignments')
      .select('programs(id, title, level, duration_weeks, cover_image_url, training_days, program_exercises(id, order_index, name, sets, reps, notes))')
      .eq('member_id', userId).eq('status', 'active')
      .order('started_at', { ascending: false }).limit(2);
    if (assignedRes.error) {
      assignedRes = await sb.from('program_assignments')
        .select('programs(id, title, level, duration_weeks, cover_image_url, program_exercises(id, order_index, name, sets, reps, notes))')
        .eq('member_id', userId).eq('status', 'active')
        .order('started_at', { ascending: false }).limit(2);
    }
    const assigned = assignedRes.data;
    // 2) Self-created programs (coach_id = user.id)
    let ownRes = await sb.from('programs')
      .select('id, title, level, duration_weeks, cover_image_url, training_days, program_exercises(id, order_index, name, sets, reps, notes)')
      .eq('coach_id', userId).order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(3);
    if (ownRes.error) {
      ownRes = await sb.from('programs')
        .select('id, title, level, duration_weeks, cover_image_url, program_exercises(id, order_index, name, sets, reps, notes)')
        .eq('coach_id', userId).order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(3);
    }
    const own = ownRes.data;
    let localOwn = [];
    try { localOwn = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.lsKey('vg_own_programs')) || '[]'); } catch (_) {}
    const assignedEntries = (assigned || []).map(r => toEntry(r.programs)).filter(Boolean);
    const ownEntries = (own || []).map(p => { const e = toEntry(p); if (e) e.subtitle = e.name + ' · Creado por ti'; return e; }).filter(Boolean);
    const all = [...assignedEntries, ...ownEntries, ...localOwn];
    // El programa "de hoy" es el que tiene el día actual entre sus días de
    // entrenamiento; los demás quedan disponibles en "Tus programas".
    const _dayNames = ['dom', 'lun', 'mar', 'mie', 'jue', 'vie', 'sab'];
    const _todayName = _dayNames[new Date().getDay()];
    const _isToday = (p) => Array.isArray(p.training_days) && p.training_days.includes(_todayName);
    const sorted = [...all].sort((a, b) => (_isToday(b) ? 1 : 0) - (_isToday(a) ? 1 : 0));
    const newReal = { ...this.state.realPrograms };
    if (sorted[0]) newReal.assigned = sorted[0];
    if (sorted[1]) newReal.assigned2 = sorted[1];
    try { localStorage.setItem(this.lsKey('vg_has_programs'), all.length ? '1' : '0'); } catch (_) {}
    this.setState({ realPrograms: newReal, assignments: sorted, programsLoaded: true });
  }

  async fetchStats() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const memberId = this.state.session.user.id;
    const { data, error } = await getSupabase()
      .from('workout_logs')
      .select('completed_at, duration_minutes')
      .eq('member_id', memberId)
      .order('completed_at', { ascending: false });
    if (error || !data) return;

    // >= 5 min = real completed session (for counts/history)
    const completedData = data.filter(w => (w.duration_minutes || 0) >= 5);
    // Toda sesión registrada cuenta — las terminadas antes del fix del mínimo
    // quedaron con 0 min y desaparecían de las estadísticas del usuario.
    const trainedData = data;
    // Count every real session (>=1 min) — the >=5 min filter made "Entrenos"
    // show 0 while "Esta semana" showed 27, since they used different data.
    const totalWorkouts = trainedData.length;
    // Total time counts ALL real activity (>=1 min) — otherwise short sessions
    // show minutes on the home screen but "0 min" total in Progress.
    const totalMinutes = trainedData.reduce((sum, w) => sum + (w.duration_minutes || 0), 0);
    // Show hours if >= 60 min, otherwise show minutes
    const totalHours = totalMinutes >= 60
      ? Math.round(totalMinutes / 60)
      : totalMinutes;
    const totalHoursUnit = totalMinutes >= 60 ? 'h' : 'min';

    // Streak: use local date key to avoid timezone mismatch
    const localDayKey = (d) => {
      const dt = new Date(d);
      return `${dt.getFullYear()}-${String(dt.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(dt.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')}`;
    };
    const dayKey = localDayKey;
    const daysWithWorkout = new Set(trainedData.map(w => localDayKey(w.completed_at)));
    const _schedDayNames = ['dom', 'lun', 'mar', 'mie', 'jue', 'vie', 'sab'];
    const _scheduledDays = this.state.memberScheduledDays || [];
    const _hasSchedule = _scheduledDays.length > 0;
    let streak = 0;
    let cursor = new Date();
    cursor.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    // If today has no workout yet, start looking from yesterday
    if (!daysWithWorkout.has(localDayKey(cursor))) {
      cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() - 1);
    }
    // Walk back up to 365 days; scheduled days must have a workout, non-scheduled days are skipped
    for (let _i = 0; _i < 365; _i++) {
      const _dayName = _schedDayNames[cursor.getDay()];
      if (!_hasSchedule || _scheduledDays.includes(_dayName)) {
        if (daysWithWorkout.has(localDayKey(cursor))) {
          streak++;
        } else {
          break;
        }
      }
      cursor.setDate(cursor.getDate() - 1);
    }

    const weekStart = new Date();
    weekStart.setDate(weekStart.getDate() - weekStart.getDay());
    weekStart.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    // Esta Semana: count = ALL workouts started this week (no duration filter)
    // time = sum of actual minutes (no minimum, so short sessions don't inflate the counter)
    const thisWeekData = trainedData.filter(w => new Date(w.completed_at) >= weekStart);
    const thisWeekCount = thisWeekData.length;
    const thisWeekMinutes = thisWeekData.reduce((sum, w) => sum + (w.duration_minutes || 0), 0);
    // Use trainedData for week dots — any activity >= 1 min marks the day
    const trainingDaysISO = new Set(
      trainedData.filter(w => new Date(w.completed_at) >= weekStart).map(w => dayKey(w.completed_at))
    );
    const weekDayNames = ['dom', 'lun', 'mar', 'mie', 'jue', 'vie', 'sab'];
    const weekDots = {};
    for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
      const d = new Date(weekStart);
      d.setDate(d.getDate() + i);
      weekDots[weekDayNames[d.getDay()]] = trainingDaysISO.has(dayKey(d));
    }

    const _fixTs = (s) => {
      if (!s) return new Date();
      const hasTz = /Z$|[+-]\d{2}:?\d{2}$/.test(s);
      return new Date(hasTz ? s : s + 'Z');
    };
    const recentLogs = trainedData.slice(0, 30).map(w => ({
      ts: _fixTs(w.completed_at).getTime(),
      date: _fixTs(w.completed_at).toLocaleDateString('es-MX', { weekday: 'short', day: 'numeric', month: 'short' }) + ' · ' + _fixTs(w.completed_at).toLocaleTimeString('es-MX', { hour: 'numeric', minute: '2-digit' }),
      duration: w.duration_minutes ? (w.duration_minutes >= 60 ? `${Math.round(w.duration_minutes/60)}h ${w.duration_minutes%60}m` : `${w.duration_minutes} min`) : '—',
    }));
    this.setState({ stats: { totalWorkouts, totalHours, totalHoursUnit, streak, thisWeekCount, thisWeekMinutes, weekDots }, recentLogs });
  }

  async fetchGymAnnouncements() {
    try {
      await waitForSupabase();
      const { data } = await getSupabase()
        .from('announcements')
        .select('title, body, image_url, created_at')
        .eq('active', true)
        .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
        .limit(1);
      this.setState({ gymAnnouncement: (data && data[0]) || null });
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  async fetchMemberProfile() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    this.fetchGymAnnouncements();
    this.fetchBranches();
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('member_profiles')
      .select('goal, level, training_days, coach_id, weight_kg, height_cm, branch_id')
      .eq('profile_id', this.state.session.user.id)
      .single();
    if (!data) return;
    const goalMap = { muscle: 'Ganar músculo', fat_loss: 'Perder grasa', health: 'Mejorar salud', performance: 'Rendimiento atlético' };
    const levelMap = { beginner: 'Principiante', intermediate: 'Intermedio', advanced: 'Avanzado' };
    this.setState({
      memberGoal: goalMap[data.goal] || data.goal || '—',
      memberLevel: levelMap[data.level] || data.level || '—',
      memberTrainingDays: data.training_days ? data.training_days.length : 0,
      memberScheduledDays: Array.isArray(data.training_days) ? data.training_days : (data.training_days ? JSON.parse(data.training_days) : []),
      memberWeight: data.weight_kg || null,
      memberHeight: data.height_cm || null,
      memberBranchId: data.branch_id || null,
    }, () => { this.checkWorkoutReminder(); });
    this.fetchBranches();
    if (data.branch_id) this.fetchCoaches();
    // Restore the assigned coach on login — without this, the coach card and
    // the chat button silently disappear on every session after onboarding.
    if (data.coach_id) {
      this.fetchCoachTip(data.coach_id);
      // El perfil del coach no es legible por RLS — usar el directorio público
      const { data: cp } = await getSupabase()
        .from('coach_profiles')
        .select('*')
        .eq('profile_id', data.coach_id)
        .single();
      if (cp) {
        const certs = Array.isArray(cp.certifications) ? cp.certifications : [];
        const nameTag = certs.find(x => typeof x === 'string' && x.indexOf('__name:') === 0);
        const avatarTag = certs.find(x => typeof x === 'string' && x.indexOf('__avatar:') === 0);
        this.setState({ assignedCoach: {
          id: data.coach_id,
          name: nameTag ? nameTag.slice(7) : 'Tu Coach',
          avatar: avatarTag && avatarTag.length > 9 ? avatarTag.slice(9) : null,
          bio: cp.bio || 'Tu entrenador asignado',
        } });
      }
    }
  }

  async saveCustomProgram() {
    const name = (this.state.cpName || '').trim();
    if (!name || !this.state.session) return;
    this.setState({ cpSaving: true });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    const cpPhotos = ["https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1534438327276-14e5300c3a48?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1517838277536-f5f99be501cd?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1540497077202-7c8a3999166f?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1583454110551-21f2fa2afe61?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1581009146145-b5ef050c2e1e?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1574680096145-d05b474e2155?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1526506118085-60ce8714f8c5?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1517836357463-d25dfeac3438?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1549060279-7e168fcee0c2?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1571019613454-1cb2f99b2d8b?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1476480862126-209bfaa8edc8?w=800&q=80","https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1544367567-0f2fcb009e0b?w=800&q=80"];
    const baseRow = {
      coach_id: this.state.session.user.id,
      title: name,
      level: 'Personalizado',
      duration_weeks: 1,
      cover_image_url: cpPhotos[this.state.cpSelectedPhotoIdx || 0],
      training_days: JSON.stringify(this.state.cpDays || []),
    };
    // Algunas columnas (duration_minutes, training_days) pueden no existir en
    // el esquema — se reintenta quitando la columna que el error señale.
    let row = { ...baseRow, duration_minutes: this.state.cpDurationMin || 45 };
    let ins = await sb.from('programs').insert(row).select('id').single();
    for (let _try = 0; _try < 3 && ins.error && /column/i.test(ins.error.message || ''); _try++) {
      const m = (ins.error.message || '').match(/'([a-z_]+)' column|column ['"]?([a-z_]+)/i);
      const badCol = m ? (m[1] || m[2]) : null;
      if (!badCol || !(badCol in row)) break;
      delete row[badCol];
      ins = await sb.from('programs').insert(row).select('id').single();
    }
    const prog = ins.data;
    if (ins.error || !prog) {
      // La base rechazó el insert (p.ej. política RLS) — guarda la rutina
      // localmente para que el usuario no pierda su trabajo.
      try {
        const own = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.lsKey('vg_own_programs')) || '[]');
        own.unshift({
          id: 'local-' + Date.now(), name, level: 'Personalizado',
          duration: String(this.state.cpDurationMin || 45),
          training_days: this.state.cpDays || [],
          cover_image_url: cpPhotos[this.state.cpSelectedPhotoIdx || 0],
          exercises: String((this.state.cpExercises || []).length),
          exerciseList: (this.state.cpExercises || []).map(ex => ({ name: ex.name, subtitle: '', setsReps: (ex.sets || '3') + ' × ' + (ex.reps || '12') })),
          subtitle: name + ' · Creado por ti',
        });
        localStorage.setItem(this.lsKey('vg_own_programs'), JSON.stringify(own.slice(0, 5)));
      } catch (_) {}
      this.setState({ cpSaving: false, createProgramOpen: false, cpName: '', cpExercises: [], cpDays: [] });
      this.setState({ workoutJustLogged: true, programToastMsg: '¡"' + name + '" guardado en este dispositivo!' });
      setTimeout(() => this.setState({ workoutJustLogged: false, programToastMsg: '' }), 3500);
      this.fetchAssignedProgram();
      return;
    }
    const exRows = this.state.cpExercises.map((ex, i) => ({
      program_id: prog.id, order_index: i,
      name: ex.name, sets: parseInt(ex.sets) || null, reps: ex.reps || null,
    }));
    if (exRows.length) await sb.from('program_exercises').insert(exRows);
    this.setState({ cpSaving: false, createProgramOpen: false, cpName: '', cpExercises: [], cpDays: [] });
    this.fetchAssignedProgram();
    const msg = `¡"${name}" creado! Ya aparece en Mis Programas.`;
    this.setState({ workoutJustLogged: true, programToastMsg: msg });
    setTimeout(() => this.setState({ workoutJustLogged: false, programToastMsg: '' }), 3500);
    this.fetchAssignedProgram();
  }

  async fetchSubscription() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('subscriptions')
      .select('status, start_date, end_date, plans(name, price)')
      .eq('member_id', this.state.session.user.id)
      .neq('status', 'canceled')
      .order('end_date', { ascending: false })
      .limit(1)
      .single();
    if (!data) return;
    const planName = data.plans ? data.plans.name : 'Plan';
    const isActive = data.status === 'active';
    const endDate = data.end_date ? new Date(data.end_date).toLocaleDateString('es-MX', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' }) : null;
    this.setState({
      subscriptionStatus: data.status,
      subscriptionPlanName: planName,
      subscriptionEndDate: endDate,
      subscriptionActive: isActive,
      subscriptionStartRaw: data.start_date || null,
      subscriptionEndRaw: data.end_date || null,
    });
  }

  async fetchCoachData() {
    if (!this.state.session || this.state.userType !== 'trainer') return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    const coachId = this.state.session.user.id;
    // Dos FKs a profiles hacían el join ambiguo (error 300) — se desambigua,
    // y si el RLS oculta el perfil del cliente, el nombre llega por el
    // mensaje de presentación (__intro) que el miembro envía al elegir coach.
    let clientsRes = await sb
      .from('member_profiles')
      .select('profile_id, goal, level, training_days, profiles!member_profiles_profile_id_fkey(full_name, email, avatar_url)')
      .eq('coach_id', coachId);
    if (clientsRes.error) {
      clientsRes = await sb
        .from('member_profiles')
        .select('profile_id, goal, level, training_days')
        .eq('coach_id', coachId);
    }
    const clients = clientsRes.data;
    if (!clients) return;
    const { count: workoutCount } = await sb
      .from('workout_logs')
      .select('id', { count: 'exact', head: true })
      .in('member_id', clients.map(c => c.profile_id));
    const { count: progCount } = await sb
      .from('programs')
      .select('id', { count: 'exact', head: true })
      .eq('coach_id', coachId);
    const _goalMap = { muscle: 'Ganar músculo', fat_loss: 'Perder grasa', health: 'Mejorar salud', performance: 'Rendimiento' };
    const _levelMap = { beginner: 'Principiante', intermediate: 'Intermedio', advanced: 'Avanzado' };
    const clientList = clients.map(c => ({
      id: c.profile_id,
      name: c.profiles?.full_name || c.profiles?.email?.split('@')[0] || 'Atleta',
      initial: ((c.profiles?.full_name || 'A')[0] || 'A').toUpperCase(),
      goal: _goalMap[c.goal] || '',
      level: _levelMap[c.level] || 'Atleta Volten',
      avatar: c.profiles?.avatar_url || null,
    }));
    this.setState({
      coachClients: clientList,
      coachStats: { clientCount: clientList.length, sessionCount: workoutCount ?? 0, programCount: progCount ?? 0 },
    }, () => { this.fetchCoachClientsToday(); this.fetchCoachClientsProgress(); this.fetchCoachMyPrograms(); this.fetchCoachSentDiets(); });
  }

  async openClientDetail(client) {
    this.setState({ ccdOpen: true, ccdClient: client, ccdProfile: null, ccdLogs: [] });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    // Trae notes (pesos) si la columna existe; si no, reintenta sin ella
    let logsRes = await sb.from('workout_logs').select('completed_at, duration_minutes, notes').eq('member_id', client.id).order('completed_at', { ascending: false }).limit(5);
    if (logsRes.error) logsRes = await sb.from('workout_logs').select('completed_at, duration_minutes').eq('member_id', client.id).order('completed_at', { ascending: false }).limit(5);
    let profRes = await sb.from('member_profiles').select('goal, level, training_days, weight_kg, height_cm, body_data').eq('profile_id', client.id).single();
    if (profRes.error) profRes = await sb.from('member_profiles').select('goal, level, training_days, weight_kg, height_cm').eq('profile_id', client.id).single();
    const prof = profRes.data;
    this.setState({ ccdProfile: prof || {}, ccdLogs: logsRes.data || [] });
  }

  async fetchCoachSentDiets() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('coach_diets')
      .select('member_id, title, content, updated_at')
      .eq('coach_id', this.state.session.user.id)
      .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(4);
    this.setState({ coachSentDiets: data || [] });
  }

  async deleteCoachProgram() {
    const p = this.state.cpdProgram;
    if (!p || !p.id) return;
    if (!confirm('¿Eliminar "' + p.title + '"? Se quitará también de los atletas que lo tienen asignado.')) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    await sb.from('program_exercises').delete().eq('program_id', p.id);
    await sb.from('program_assignments').delete().eq('program_id', p.id);
    await sb.from('programs').delete().eq('id', p.id);
    this.setState({ cpdOpen: false });
    this.showToast('Programa eliminado');
    this.fetchCoachData();
  }

  async openCoachProgramDetail(p) {
    this.setState({ cpdOpen: true, cpdProgram: p, cpdExs: [], cpdAssignees: [] });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    const [{ data: exs }, { data: asg }] = await Promise.all([
      sb.from('program_exercises').select('name, sets, reps, order_index').eq('program_id', p.id).order('order_index'),
      sb.from('program_assignments').select('member_id, started_at').eq('program_id', p.id),
    ]);
    const clients = this.state.coachClients || [];
    const assignees = (asg || []).map(a2 => {
      const c = clients.find(x => x.id === a2.member_id);
      return {
        name: c ? c.name : 'Atleta',
        initial: c ? c.initial : 'A',
        avatar: c ? c.avatar : null,
        when: a2.started_at ? new Date(/Z$|[+-]\d{2}:?\d{2}$/.test(a2.started_at) ? a2.started_at : (a2.started_at + 'Z')).toLocaleDateString('es-MX', { day: 'numeric', month: 'short', hour: 'numeric', minute: '2-digit' }) : '',
      };
    });
    this.setState({ cpdExs: exs || [], cpdAssignees: assignees });
  }

  async fetchCoachMyPrograms() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('programs')
      .select('id, title, level, training_days, cover_image_url')
      .eq('coach_id', this.state.session.user.id)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(4);
    this.setState({ coachMyPrograms: data || [] });
  }

  async fetchCoachClientsProgress() {
    const ids = (this.state.coachClients || []).map(c => c.id);
    if (!ids.length) { this.setState({ coachClientProg: {}, coachTodayAgg: { sessions: 0, minutes: 0 } }); return; }
    await waitForSupabase();
    const weekStart = new Date();
    weekStart.setDate(weekStart.getDate() - weekStart.getDay());
    weekStart.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('workout_logs')
      .select('member_id, completed_at, duration_minutes')
      .in('member_id', ids)
      .gte('completed_at', weekStart.toISOString());
    const prog = {};
    let tS = 0, tM = 0;
    const todayKey = new Date().toDateString();
    (data || []).forEach(w => {
      const p = prog[w.member_id] = prog[w.member_id] || { week: 0, min: 0, last: null };
      p.week++; p.min += w.duration_minutes || 0;
      const d = new Date(/Z$|[+-]\d{2}:?\d{2}$/.test(w.completed_at || '') ? w.completed_at : (w.completed_at + 'Z'));
      if (!p.last || d > p.last) p.last = d;
      if (d.toDateString() === todayKey) { tS++; tM += w.duration_minutes || 0; }
    });
    this.setState({ coachClientProg: prog, coachTodayAgg: { sessions: tS, minutes: tM } });
  }

  // Publica la ficha pública del coach en coach_profiles (nombre + foto),
  // que es la única tabla que los miembros pueden leer para elegir coach.
  // Mensaje oculto para que el coach conozca el nombre del atleta
  // (el RLS de profiles no deja leer nombres ajenos).
  // Último consejo del coach para mostrarlo en el home del atleta
  async fetchCoachTip(coachId) {
    try {
      await waitForSupabase();
      const { data } = await getSupabase().from('coach_profiles').select('certifications').eq('profile_id', coachId).single();
      const certs = Array.isArray(data && data.certifications) ? data.certifications : [];
      const tag = certs.find(x => typeof x === 'string' && x.indexOf('__tip:') === 0);
      if (tag) {
        const raw = tag.slice(6);
        const text = raw.lastIndexOf('|') > -1 ? raw.slice(0, raw.lastIndexOf('|')) : raw;
        this.setState({ memberCoachTip: text });
      }
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  // El nombre y la foto del atleta ya viajan por el join directo de
  // fetchCoachData — no se necesita ningún mensaje de presentación.
  async sendIntroToCoach(coachId) { return; }

  async syncCoachDirectory(session) {
    try {
      await waitForSupabase();
      const sb = getSupabase();
      const uid = session.user.id;
      const meta = session.user.user_metadata || {};
      const name = meta.full_name || 'Entrenador';
      let avatar = null;
      try { avatar = localStorage.getItem('vg_avatar_' + uid) || meta.avatar_url || null; } catch (_) {}
      sb.from('profiles').update({ role: 'coach' }).eq('id', uid).then(() => {});
      const certs = ['__name:' + name];
      if (avatar) certs.push('__avatar:' + avatar);
      await sb.from('coach_profiles').upsert({ profile_id: uid, certifications: certs }, { onConflict: 'profile_id' });
      this.fetchCoaches();
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  async removeCoach() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    if (!confirm('¿Quitar a tu entrenador? Podrás elegir otro (o el mismo) cuando quieras.')) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    await getSupabase().from('member_profiles').update({ coach_id: null }).eq('profile_id', this.state.session.user.id);
    this.setState({ assignedCoach: null, memberCoachTip: null });
    this.showToast('Entrenador removido');
  }

  async saveCoachFromProfile() {
    const cid = this.state.selectedCoachId;
    if (!cid || !this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { error } = await getSupabase()
      .from('member_profiles')
      .upsert({ profile_id: this.state.session.user.id, coach_id: cid }, { onConflict: 'profile_id' });
    if (error) { alert('No se pudo guardar tu coach: ' + error.message); return; }
    const c = (this.state.coaches || []).find(x => x.id === cid);
    if (c) this.sendPosRequest('coach', c.id, c.name, parseFloat(String(c.price || '').replace(/[^0-9.]/g, '')) || null);
    this.setState({ coachPickerOpen: false });
    if (c) alert('Solicitud enviada. Tu entrenador ' + c.name + ' queda PENDIENTE de pago — pasa a recepción a pagarlo (' + (c.price || 'precio en recepcion') + '). Aparecerá como tu coach en cuanto se registre el pago.');
  }

  async coachAssignProgram() {
    const nameEl = document.getElementById('cw-name');
    const name = ((nameEl && nameEl.value) || this.state.coachAssignProgramName || '').trim();
    const ids = this.state.cwClientIds || [];
    if (!ids.length) { alert('Elige al menos un atleta.'); return; }
    if (!name) { alert('Ponle nombre al programa.'); return; }
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    this.setState({ coachAssignSaving: true });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    const caPhotos = [
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1534438327276-14e5300c3a48?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1517838277536-f5f99be501cd?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1540497077202-7c8a3999166f?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1583454110551-21f2fa2afe61?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1581009146145-b5ef050c2e1e?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1574680096145-d05b474e2155?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1549060279-7e168fcee0c2?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1571019613454-1cb2f99b2d8b?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1526506118085-60ce8714f8c5?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1476480862126-209bfaa8edc8?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1518611012118-696072aa579a?w=800&q=80',
      'https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1544367567-0f2fcb009e0b?w=800&q=80',
    ];
    let progRow = {
      coach_id: this.state.session.user.id, title: name,
      level: this.state.coachAssignLevel || 'Intermedio',
      cover_image_url: caPhotos[this.state.caSelectedPhotoIdx || 0],
      duration_minutes: this.state.caDurationMin || 45,
      training_days: JSON.stringify(this.state.coachAssignDays || []),
    };
    let progRes = await sb.from('programs').insert(progRow).select('id').single();
    for (let _try = 0; _try < 3 && progRes.error && /column/i.test(progRes.error.message || ''); _try++) {
      const m = (progRes.error.message || '').match(/'([a-z_]+)' column|column ['"]?([a-z_]+)/i);
      const badCol = m ? (m[1] || m[2]) : null;
      if (!badCol || !(badCol in progRow)) break;
      delete progRow[badCol];
      progRes = await sb.from('programs').insert(progRow).select('id').single();
    }
    const prog = progRes.data;
    if (!prog) { this.setState({ coachAssignSaving: false }); alert('No se pudo asignar: ' + (progRes.error ? progRes.error.message : 'error desconocido')); return; }
    const picked = this.state.coachAssignPicked || [];
    if (picked.length) {
      const exRows = picked.map((ex, i) => {
        const parts = ex.r.split('×').map(s => s.trim());
        return { program_id: prog.id, order_index: i, name: ex.n, sets: parts.length > 1 ? parseInt(parts[0]) || null : null, reps: parts.length > 1 ? parts[1] : ex.r };
      });
      await sb.from('program_exercises').insert(exRows);
    }
    // El mismo programa se asigna a TODOS los atletas seleccionados
    for (const clientId of ids) {
      await sb.from('program_assignments').insert({ program_id: prog.id, member_id: clientId, assigned_by: this.state.session.user.id, status: 'active' });
    }
    if (nameEl) nameEl.value = '';
    this.setState({
      coachAssignSaving: false, coachAssignProgramName: '', coachAssignLevel: '',
      coachAssignDays: [], coachAssignPicked: [], caSelectedPhotoIdx: 0, caDurationMin: 45,
      cwOpen: false, cwClientIds: [],
    });
    this.showToast('"' + name + '" asignado a ' + ids.length + ' atleta' + (ids.length > 1 ? 's' : '') + ' ✓');
    this.fetchCoachData();
  }

  async coachSendDiet() {
    const ids = this.state.cwClientIds || [];
    const readEl = (id) => { const el = document.getElementById(id); return el ? el.value.trim() : ''; };
    const title = readEl('cw-diet-name') || 'Plan alimenticio';
    const mealBlock = (label, o1, o2) => {
      if (!o1 && !o2) return '';
      let s = label + ':';
      if (o1) s += '\n  Opción 1: ' + o1;
      if (o2) s += '\n  Opción 2: ' + o2;
      return s;
    };
    const meals = [
      mealBlock('Desayuno', readEl('cw-m-b1'), readEl('cw-m-b2')),
      mealBlock('Comida', readEl('cw-m-l1'), readEl('cw-m-l2')),
      mealBlock('Cena', readEl('cw-m-d1'), readEl('cw-m-d2')),
      mealBlock('Snacks', readEl('cw-m-s1'), readEl('cw-m-s2')),
    ].filter(Boolean);
    const days = this.state.coachDietDays || [];
    const weeks = this.state.cdDurationWeeks || 1;
    const header = (days.length ? 'Días: ' + days.map(d => d.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + d.slice(1)).join(', ') + '\n' : '') + 'Duración: ' + weeks + (weeks > 1 ? ' semanas' : ' semana');
    const content = (header + '\n\n' + meals.join('\n\n')).trim();
    if (!ids.length) { alert('Elige al menos un atleta.'); return; }
    if (!meals.length) { alert('Escribe al menos una comida.'); return; }
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    this.setState({ coachDietSaving: true });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    let lastErr = null;
    for (const clientId of ids) {
      // La tabla no tiene constraint único (coach_id, member_id): borrar e insertar
      await sb.from('coach_diets').delete().match({ coach_id: this.state.session.user.id, member_id: clientId });
      const { error } = await sb.from('coach_diets').insert({
        coach_id: this.state.session.user.id, member_id: clientId, title, content,
        updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      });
      if (error) lastErr = error;
    }
    this.setState({ coachDietSaving: false });
    if (lastErr) { alert('No se pudo enviar: ' + lastErr.message); return; }
    this.showToast('Dieta enviada a ' + ids.length + ' atleta' + (ids.length > 1 ? 's' : '') + ' ✓');
    ['cw-diet-name','cw-m-b1','cw-m-b2','cw-m-l1','cw-m-l2','cw-m-d1','cw-m-d2','cw-m-s1','cw-m-s2'].forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.value = ''; });
    this.setState({ cwOpen: false, cwClientIds: [], coachDietDays: [], cdDurationWeeks: 1 });
  }

  async fetchMemberDiet() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('coach_diets')
      .select('title, content, updated_at')
      .eq('member_id', this.state.session.user.id)
      .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(1)
      .single();
    if (data) this.setState({ memberDiet: data });
  }

  async fetchCoachClientsToday() {
    if (!this.state.session || this.state.userType !== 'trainer') return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    // El día se calcula en hora LOCAL — con UTC salían sesiones de ayer
    const dayStart = new Date(); dayStart.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    const dayEnd = new Date(dayStart.getTime() + 86400000);
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('workout_logs')
      .select('member_id, completed_at, duration_minutes, programs(title), profiles!member_id(full_name)')
      .gte('completed_at', dayStart.toISOString())
      .lt('completed_at', dayEnd.toISOString())
      .in('member_id', this.state.coachClients.map(c => c.id) || []);
    this.setState({ coachTodaySessions: data || [] });
  }



  async fetchFavorites() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('favorites')
      .select('program_id, programs(id, title, level, cover_image_url, slug)')
      .eq('member_id', this.state.session.user.id);
    if (!data) return;
    const favIds = data.map(f => f.program_id).filter(Boolean);
    const favPrograms = data.map(f => f.programs).filter(Boolean);
    this.setState({ favProgramIds: favIds, favProgramDetails: favPrograms });
  }

  async toggleFavorite(programId) {
    if (!this.state.session || !programId) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    const favIds = Array.isArray(this.state.favProgramIds) ? this.state.favProgramIds : [];
    if (favIds.includes(programId)) {
      await sb.from('favorites').delete().match({ member_id: this.state.session.user.id, program_id: programId });
      this.setState({ favProgramIds: favIds.filter(id => id !== programId) });
    } else {
      await sb.from('favorites').insert({ member_id: this.state.session.user.id, program_id: programId });
      this.setState({ favProgramIds: [...favIds, programId] });
    }
    this.fetchFavorites();
  }

  toggleLocalFav(slug) {
    const arr = Array.isArray(this.state.localFavSlugs) ? this.state.localFavSlugs : [];
    const removing = arr.includes(slug);
    const next = removing ? arr.filter(s => s !== slug) : [...arr, slug];
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(this.lsKey('vg_favs'), JSON.stringify(next));
      if (removing) {
        // Al quitar el corazón también desaparece de "recientes" del home
        const rec = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.lsKey('vg_recents')) || '[]').filter(s => s !== slug);
        localStorage.setItem(this.lsKey('vg_recents'), JSON.stringify(rec));
      }
    } catch (_) {}
    this.setState({ localFavSlugs: next });
  }

  async fetchPersonalRecords() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data, error } = await getSupabase()
      .from('personal_records')
      .select('id, exercise_name, value, unit, achieved_at')
      .eq('member_id', this.state.session.user.id)
      .order('achieved_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(5);
    let localPrs = [];
    try { localPrs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('vg_prs') || '[]'); } catch (_) {}
    this.setState({ personalRecords: [...localPrs, ...((!error && data) ? data : [])].slice(0, 5) });
  }

  async fetchCuratedExercises() {
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase().from('exercise_catalog').select('name, category, muscle_groups, equipment').order('name');
    if (!data || !data.length) return;
    const grouped = {};
    data.forEach(ex => {
      const cat = ex.category;
      if (!grouped[cat]) grouped[cat] = [];
      grouped[cat].push({ name: ex.name, subtitle: ex.muscle_groups || '', setsReps: '3 × 12' });
    });
    this.setState({ curatedExercises: grouped });
  }

  async fetchProgressPhotos() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('progress_photos')
      .select('id, photo_url, note, taken_at')
      .eq('member_id', this.state.session.user.id)
      .order('taken_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(12);
    let localPh = [];
    try { localPh = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('vg_photos') || '[]'); } catch (_) {}
    this.setState({ progressPhotos: [...localPh, ...(data || [])].slice(0, 12) });
  }

  // Downscale + JPEG-compress an image file to a data URL. Keeps rows small
  // enough to live directly in the progress_photos table (no Storage bucket
  // needed — the bucket was never provisioned and uploads always failed).
  compressImage(file, maxDim, quality) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const img = new Image();
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);
      img.onload = () => {
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
        const scale = Math.min(1, maxDim / Math.max(img.width, img.height));
        const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
        canvas.width = Math.round(img.width * scale);
        canvas.height = Math.round(img.height * scale);
        canvas.getContext('2d').drawImage(img, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
        resolve(canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', quality));
      };
      img.onerror = () => { URL.revokeObjectURL(url); reject(new Error('No se pudo leer la imagen')); };
      img.src = url;
    });
  }

  uploadProgressPhoto() {
    const input = document.createElement('input');
    input.type = 'file';
    input.accept = 'image/*';
    input.onchange = async (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if (!file || !this.state.session) return;
      this.setState({ photoUploading: true });
      try {
        const dataUrl = await this.compressImage(file, 900, 0.72);
        await waitForSupabase();
        const { error } = await getSupabase().from('progress_photos').insert({
          member_id: this.state.session.user.id,
          photo_url: dataUrl,
        });
        if (error) {
          // Respaldo local: la foto vive en el dispositivo
          const local = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('vg_photos') || '[]');
          local.unshift({ id: 'local-' + Date.now(), photo_url: dataUrl, taken_at: new Date().toISOString() });
          localStorage.setItem('vg_photos', JSON.stringify(local.slice(0, 4)));
        }
        this.fetchProgressPhotos();
      } catch (err) {
        alert('No se pudo guardar la foto: ' + err.message);
      }
      this.setState({ photoUploading: false });
    };
    input.click();
  }

  uploadAvatar() {
    const input = document.createElement('input');
    input.type = 'file';
    input.accept = 'image/*';
    input.onchange = async (e) => {
      const file = e.target.files[0];
      if (!file || !this.state.session) return;
      this.setState({ avatarUploading: true });
      try {
        // Small square avatar stored in auth user_metadata — no extra tables.
        const dataUrl = await this.compressImage(file, 256, 0.8);
        await waitForSupabase();
        const { error } = await getSupabase().auth.updateUser({ data: { avatar_url: dataUrl } });
        if (error) throw new Error(error.message);
        // También en profiles.avatar_url — así los coaches salen con foto
        // en la pantalla de "elige tu entrenador".
        getSupabase().from('profiles').update({ avatar_url: dataUrl }).eq('id', this.state.session.user.id).then(() => {});
        try { localStorage.setItem('vg_avatar_' + this.state.session.user.id, dataUrl); } catch (_) {}
        if (this.state.userType === 'trainer') this.syncCoachDirectory(this.state.session);
        this.setState({ userAvatar: dataUrl });
      } catch (err) {
        alert('No se pudo guardar la foto de perfil: ' + err.message);
      }
      this.setState({ avatarUploading: false });
    };
    input.click();
  }

  async openChat(partnerId, partnerName) {
    this.setState({ chatOpen: true, chatPartnerId: partnerId, chatPartnerName: partnerName, chatMessages: [] });
    this.fetchMessages(partnerId);
  }

  async fetchMessages(partnerId) {
    if (!this.state.session || !partnerId) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const uid = this.state.session.user.id;
    const { data } = await getSupabase()
      .from('messages')
      .select('id, from_id, to_id, body, created_at, read')
      .or(`and(from_id.eq.${uid},to_id.eq.${partnerId}),and(from_id.eq.${partnerId},to_id.eq.${uid})`)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: true })
      .limit(50);
    if (data) this.setState({ chatMessages: data.filter(m => !(m.body || '').startsWith('__intro')) });
    // Mark received as read
    await getSupabase().from('messages').update({ read: true }).eq('to_id', uid).eq('from_id', partnerId).eq('read', false);
    this.fetchUnreadCount();
  }

  async sendMessage() {
    const body = (this.state.chatInput || '').trim();
    if (!body || !this.state.session || !this.state.chatPartnerId) return;
    this.setState({ chatSending: true, chatInput: '' });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { error } = await getSupabase().from('messages').insert({ from_id: this.state.session.user.id, to_id: this.state.chatPartnerId, body });
    this.setState({ chatSending: false });
    if (error) { alert('No se pudo enviar el mensaje: ' + error.message); this.setState({ chatInput: body }); return; }
    this.fetchMessages(this.state.chatPartnerId);
  }

  showToast(msg) {
    this.setState({ workoutJustLogged: true, programToastMsg: msg });
    clearTimeout(this._toastTimer);
    this._toastTimer = setTimeout(() => this.setState({ workoutJustLogged: false, programToastMsg: '' }), 3200);
  }

  async sendCoachTip() {
    const body = (this.state.coachTipInput || '').trim();
    const clients = this.state.coachClients || [];
    if (!body) { alert('Escribe el consejo antes de enviarlo.'); return; }
    if (!clients.length) { alert('Aún no tienes atletas a quién enviárselo.'); return; }
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    this.setState({ coachTipSending: true });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const sb = getSupabase();
    const { data: cp } = await sb.from('coach_profiles').select('certifications').eq('profile_id', this.state.session.user.id).single();
    const kept = (cp && Array.isArray(cp.certifications) ? cp.certifications : []).filter(x => typeof x !== 'string' || x.indexOf('__tip:') !== 0);
    kept.push('__tip:' + body + '|' + Date.now());
    const { error } = await sb.from('coach_profiles').upsert({ profile_id: this.state.session.user.id, certifications: kept }, { onConflict: 'profile_id' });
    this.setState({ coachTipSending: false });
    if (error) { alert('No se pudo enviar: ' + error.message); return; }
    this.setState({ coachTipInput: '' });
    const _tipEl = document.getElementById('coach-tip-input');
    if (_tipEl) _tipEl.value = '';
    this.showToast('Consejo enviado a tus atletas ✓');
  }

  async fetchUnreadCount() {
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { count } = await getSupabase()
      .from('messages')
      .select('id', { count: 'exact', head: true })
      .eq('to_id', this.state.session.user.id)
      .eq('read', false)
      .not('body', 'like', '\\_\\_intro:%');
    this.setState({ unreadMessages: count || 0 });
  }

  async addPersonalRecord() {
    const name = (this.state.newPrName || '').trim();
    const value = parseFloat(this.state.newPrValue);
    if (!name || !value || !this.state.session) return;
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { error } = await getSupabase().from('personal_records').insert({
      member_id: this.state.session.user.id,
      exercise_name: name,
      value,
      unit: 'kg',
    });
    if (error) {
      // Guarda el récord localmente si la base lo rechaza
      try {
        const local = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('vg_prs') || '[]');
        local.unshift({ id: 'local-' + Date.now(), exercise_name: name, value, unit: 'kg', achieved_at: new Date().toISOString() });
        localStorage.setItem('vg_prs', JSON.stringify(local.slice(0, 10)));
      } catch (_) {}
      this.setState({ newPrName: '', newPrValue: '', addingPr: false, personalRecords: [{ id: 'local', exercise_name: name, value, unit: 'kg', achieved_at: new Date().toISOString() }, ...this.state.personalRecords].slice(0, 5) });
      return;
    }
    if (!error) {
      this.setState({ newPrName: '', newPrValue: '', addingPr: false });
      this.fetchPersonalRecords();
    }
  }

  async componentDidMount() {
    await waitForSupabase();
    const supabaseClient = getSupabase();
    const { data } = await supabaseClient.auth.getSession();
    // Page-load restore (or a Google OAuth redirect bouncing back) always
    // jumps straight into the app — this is an existing session, not a
    // fresh signup, so the onboarding questionnaire should not show again.
    if (data.session) this.applySession(data.session);
    this.setupManualScroll();
    this.fetchCoaches();
    this.fetchPrograms();
    this.fetchCuratedExercises();
    // Restore diet streak from localStorage
    try {
      const _vgd = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('vg_diet') || '{}');
      const _today = new Date().toDateString();
      const _sameDay = _vgd.lastMealDate === _today;
      this.setState({
        dietStreak: _vgd.streak || 0,
        dietLastFollowDate: _vgd.lastFollowDate || '',
        dietMealB: _sameDay ? !!_vgd.mealB : false,
        dietMealL: _sameDay ? !!_vgd.mealL : false,
        dietMealD: _sameDay ? !!_vgd.mealD : false,
        dietMealS: _sameDay ? !!_vgd.mealS : false,
      });
    } catch(_) {}
  }

  componentWillUnmount() {
    clearInterval(this._timerInterval);
  }

  checkWorkoutReminder() {
    try {
      const sched = this.state.memberScheduledDays || [];
      if (!sched.length) return;
      const dayNames = ['dom','lun','mar','mie','jue','vie','sab'];
      const todayName = dayNames[new Date().getDay()];
      if (!sched.includes(todayName)) return;
      const dots = this.state.stats.weekDots || {};
      if (dots[todayName]) return; // Ya entrenó hoy
      // Solo mostrar el banner una vez por día (no en cada apertura de la app)
      const _todayStr = new Date().toDateString();
      if (localStorage.getItem('vg_banner_date') === _todayStr) return;
      localStorage.setItem('vg_banner_date', _todayStr);
      // Notificación del sistema SOLO si el usuario ya la otorgó previamente
      // (nunca pedimos permiso automáticamente — eso es intrusivo)
      if (!('Notification' in window)) return;
      if (Notification.permission !== 'granted') return;
      try {
        new Notification('Volten Gym — Hoy toca entrenar', {
          body: 'Tu rutina te espera. Mantén tu racha activa.',
          tag: 'volten-reminder',
          renotify: false,
        });
      } catch (_) {}
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  // Desktop Chrome, in this deeply-nested flex + overflow-auto layout, was
  // not reliably routing wheel/keyboard scroll to the correct nested
  // scrollable container (touch scroll worked fine, proving the container
  // itself is scrollable — the browser's automatic wheel/key scroll target
  // resolution was the broken part). Handle both manually instead of
  // relying on native scroll-chaining.
  setupManualScroll() {
    const findScrollTarget = () => {
      const root = document.getElementById('app-root');
      if (!root) return null;
      const onb = root.querySelector('x-dc, [data-dc-tpl]');
      // Prefer the currently visible onboarding step if onboarding overlay is showing.
      const all = [...root.querySelectorAll('div')];
      const visible = all.filter(d => {
        const cs = getComputedStyle(d);
        return (cs.overflowY === 'auto' || cs.overflowY === 'scroll') && d.clientHeight > 0 && cs.display !== 'none';
      });
      return visible.find(d => d.scrollHeight > d.clientHeight) || visible[0] || null;
    };

    // A horizontal scroller under the cursor takes priority over the manual
    // vertical routing — otherwise the preventDefault below kills sideways
    // wheel/trackpad scroll on carousels.
    const findHScroller = (start) => {
      let el = start;
      while (el && el.nodeType === 1 && el !== document.body) {
        const cs = getComputedStyle(el);
        if ((cs.overflowX === 'auto' || cs.overflowX === 'scroll') && el.scrollWidth > el.clientWidth + 2) return el;
        el = el.parentElement;
      }
      return null;
    };

    document.addEventListener('wheel', (e) => {
      const h = findHScroller(e.target);
      if (h) {
        h.scrollLeft += (Math.abs(e.deltaX) > Math.abs(e.deltaY) ? e.deltaX : e.deltaY);
        e.preventDefault();
        return;
      }
      const target = findScrollTarget();
      if (!target) return;
      target.scrollTop += e.deltaY;
      e.preventDefault();
    }, { passive: false });

    // Drag-to-scroll for horizontal carousels — mouse AND touch. Touch needs
    // it too: tap handling on the cards was eating the native horizontal pan,
    // so we scroll the container manually from pointer moves.
    document.addEventListener('pointerdown', (e) => {
      if (e.pointerType === 'mouse' && e.button !== 0) return;
      const scroller = findHScroller(e.target);
      if (!scroller) return;
      const startX = e.clientX;
      const startY = e.clientY;
      const startLeft = scroller.scrollLeft;
      let dragged = false;
      let vertical = false;
      const onMove = (ev) => {
        const dx = ev.clientX - startX;
        const dy = ev.clientY - startY;
        // A clearly vertical gesture belongs to the page scroll — let it go.
        if (!dragged && !vertical && Math.abs(dy) > 10 && Math.abs(dy) > Math.abs(dx) * 1.5) { vertical = true; return; }
        if (vertical) return;
        if (Math.abs(dx) > 6) dragged = true;
        if (dragged) scroller.scrollLeft = startLeft - dx;
      };
      const cleanup = () => {
        document.removeEventListener('pointermove', onMove);
        document.removeEventListener('pointerup', cleanup);
        document.removeEventListener('pointercancel', cleanup);
        if (dragged) {
          const swallow = (ce) => { ce.stopPropagation(); ce.preventDefault(); };
          document.addEventListener('click', swallow, true);
          setTimeout(() => document.removeEventListener('click', swallow, true), 120);
        }
      };
      document.addEventListener('pointermove', onMove);
      document.addEventListener('pointerup', cleanup);
      document.addEventListener('pointercancel', cleanup);
    });

    document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      const tag = document.activeElement && document.activeElement.tagName;
      if (tag === 'INPUT' || tag === 'TEXTAREA') return;
      const target = findScrollTarget();
      if (!target) return;
      const step = 60;
      if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') { target.scrollTop += step; e.preventDefault(); }
      else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') { target.scrollTop -= step; e.preventDefault(); }
      else if (e.key === 'PageDown' || e.key === ' ') { target.scrollTop += target.clientHeight * 0.85; e.preventDefault(); }
      else if (e.key === 'PageUp') { target.scrollTop -= target.clientHeight * 0.85; e.preventDefault(); }
      else if (e.key === 'Home') { target.scrollTop = 0; e.preventDefault(); }
      else if (e.key === 'End') { target.scrollTop = target.scrollHeight; e.preventDefault(); }
    });
  }

  applySession(session) {
    this._appliedSessionUserId = session.user.id;
    const meta = session.user.user_metadata || {};
    this.setState({
      session,
      userName: meta.full_name || this.state.userName,
      userAvatar: (() => { try { return localStorage.getItem('vg_avatar_' + session.user.id) || meta.avatar_url || null; } catch (_) { return meta.avatar_url || null; } })(),
      userEmail: session.user.email || this.state.userEmail,
      userType: meta.role === 'coach' ? 'trainer' : 'member',
      onboardingStep: 8,
      screen: meta.role === 'coach' ? 'coach' : 'home',
      authError: '',
      authLoading: false,
    });
    try {
      // Migración: datos guardados antes de separar por usuario
      ['vg_favs', 'vg_own_programs', 'vg_recents'].forEach(k => {
        const scoped = this.lsKey(k);
        if (!localStorage.getItem(scoped) && localStorage.getItem(k)) {
          localStorage.setItem(scoped, localStorage.getItem(k));
          localStorage.removeItem(k);
        }
      });
      const _favs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.lsKey('vg_favs')) || '[]');
      this.setState({ localFavSlugs: Array.isArray(_favs) ? _favs : [] });
    } catch (_) {}
    if (meta.role === 'coach') {
      this.syncCoachDirectory(session);
    }
    this.fetchCoaches();
    this.fetchStats();
    this.fetchPersonalRecords();
    this.fetchMemberProfile();
    this.fetchAssignedProgram();
    this.fetchSubscription();
    this.fetchCoachData();
    this.fetchMemberDiet();
    this.fetchFavorites();
    this.fetchProgressPhotos();
    this.fetchUnreadCount();
  }

  async signUpWithEmail() {
    const { userEmail, userPassword, userName, userType } = this.state;
    if (!userEmail || !userPassword) {
      this.setState({ authError: 'Completa correo y contraseña.' });
      return;
    }
    this.setState({ authLoading: true, authError: '' });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const { data, error } = await getSupabase().auth.signUp({
      email: userEmail,
      password: userPassword,
      options: {
        data: {
          full_name: userName,
          role: 'member', // los entrenadores los da de alta el administrador
        },
      },
    });
    if (error) {
      this.setState({ authLoading: false, authError: error.message });
      return;
    }
    if (data.session) { this._appliedSessionUserId = data.session.user.id; this.fetchCoaches(); this.fetchBranches(); }
    // A brand-new account continues into the onboarding questionnaire
    // (goal / level / training days) instead of jumping to the home screen.
    this.setState(s => ({
      session: data.session,
      authLoading: false,
      onboardingStep: s.onboardingStep + 1,
    }));
  }

  async loginWithEmail() {
    // login por usuario o correo: coaches/staff pueden teclear solo su usuario
    const { userEmail, userPassword } = this.state;
    if (!userEmail || !userPassword) {
      this.setState({ authError: 'Completa usuario y contraseña.' });
      return;
    }
    this.setState({ authLoading: true, authError: '' });
    await waitForSupabase();
    const raw = String(userEmail).trim();
    const tries = raw.indexOf('@') !== -1 ? [raw] : [raw + '@volten.pos', raw + '@volten.app', raw + '@gmail.com'];
    let data = null, error = null;
    for (const em of tries) {
      const r = await getSupabase().auth.signInWithPassword({ email: em, password: userPassword });
      if (!r.error) { data = r.data; error = null; break; }
      error = r.error;
    }
    if (error) {
      this.setState({ authLoading: false, authError: 'Usuario o contraseña incorrectos.' });
      return;
    }
    if (data.session) this.applySession(data.session);
  }

  runScrollDiag() {
    const root = document.getElementById('app-root');
    if (!root) { alert('NO se encontró #app-root'); return; }
    const all = [...root.querySelectorAll('div')];
    const scrollable = all.filter(d => {
      const cs = getComputedStyle(d);
      return (cs.overflowY === 'auto' || cs.overflowY === 'scroll');
    });
    const visible = scrollable.filter(d => d.clientHeight > 0 && getComputedStyle(d).display !== 'none');
    const target = visible.find(d => d.scrollHeight > d.clientHeight) || visible[0];
    let hitInfo = 'no target';
    let beforeScroll = 'n/a';
    let afterScroll = 'n/a';
    let wheelDefaultPrevented = 'n/a';
    if (target) {
      const r = target.getBoundingClientRect();
      const cx = r.left + r.width / 2;
      const cy = r.top + r.height / 2;
      const hit = document.elementFromPoint(cx, cy);
      const isInsideTarget = target.contains(hit);
      hitInfo = `hitTag=${hit ? hit.tagName : 'null'} isInsideScrollTarget=${isInsideTarget} hitText="${hit ? hit.textContent.slice(0,25) : ''}"`;
      beforeScroll = String(target.scrollTop);
      const ev = new WheelEvent('wheel', { deltaY: 150, bubbles: true, cancelable: true, clientX: cx, clientY: cy });
      const notPrevented = target.dispatchEvent(ev);
      wheelDefaultPrevented = String(!notPrevented);
      afterScroll = String(target.scrollTop);
    }
    const lines = visible.map((d, i) => `#${i}: h=${d.clientHeight} scrollH=${d.scrollHeight} canScroll=${d.scrollHeight > d.clientHeight}`);
    const ua = navigator.userAgent;

    // Walk from target up to root: report pointer-events / touch-action / overflow at each level.
    let chainLines = [];
    if (target) {
      let el = target;
      let depth = 0;
      while (el && depth < 8) {
        const cs = getComputedStyle(el);
        chainLines.push(`${depth}:<${el.tagName.toLowerCase()}> pe=${cs.pointerEvents} ta=${cs.touchAction} ov=${cs.overflow} pos=${cs.position} z=${cs.zIndex}`);
        if (el === root) break;
        el = el.parentElement;
        depth++;
      }
    }

    // Look for any large invisible overlay covering most of #app-root with pointer-events not none.
    const rootR = root.getBoundingClientRect();
    const overlays = [...root.querySelectorAll('*')].filter(el => {
      const cs = getComputedStyle(el);
      if (cs.position !== 'fixed' && cs.position !== 'absolute') return false;
      if (cs.pointerEvents === 'none') return false;
      if (cs.display === 'none') return false;
      const r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
      return r.width >= rootR.width * 0.7 && r.height >= rootR.height * 0.7;
    });
    const overlayLines = overlays.map(el => `<${el.tagName.toLowerCase()}> z=${getComputedStyle(el).zIndex} opacity=${getComputedStyle(el).opacity} bg=${getComputedStyle(el).backgroundColor}`);

    alert(
      'DIAGNÓSTICO\n' + 'screen=' + this.state.screen + '\n' + lines.join('\n') +
      '\n\n' + hitInfo +
      '\nscrollTop antes=' + beforeScroll + ' después=' + afterScroll +
      '\nwheelEvent.preventDefault llamado=' + wheelDefaultPrevented +
      '\n\nCADENA (target -> root):\n' + chainLines.join('\n') +
      '\n\nOVERLAYS GRANDES ENCONTRADOS (' + overlays.length + '):\n' + overlayLines.join('\n') +
      '\n\nUA: ' + ua
    );
  }

  // Reinicia las animaciones de entrada cada vez que cambias de pestaña,
  // para que cada pantalla "cobre vida" al entrar (no solo al cargar la app).
  replayAnims() {
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      const els = document.querySelectorAll('.vg-s0, .vg-s1, .vg-s2, .vg-s3, .vg-s4, .vg-s5');
      els.forEach(el => {
        el.style.animation = 'none';
        void el.offsetHeight;
        el.style.animation = '';
      });
    });
  }

  // Claves de localStorage separadas por usuario — sin esto, los favoritos y
  // rutinas locales de una cuenta aparecían al iniciar sesión con otra.
  lsKey(name) {
    const uid = this.state.session ? this.state.session.user.id.slice(0, 8) : 'anon';
    return name + '_' + uid;
  }

  async signOut() {
    await waitForSupabase();
    await getSupabase().auth.signOut();
    this._appliedSessionUserId = null;
    // Reset every per-account field — leftover stats/profile data from the
    // previous account was staying on screen until the new account's fetch
    // completed, making a brand-new account look like it had history.
    this.setState({
      session: null,
      onboardingStep: 0,
      screen: 'home',
      userName: '',
      userEmail: '',
      userPassword: '',
      authError: '',
      authMode: 'signup',
      stats: { totalWorkouts: 0, totalHours: 0, totalHoursUnit: 'h', streak: 0, thisWeekCount: 0, weekDots: {} },
      recentLogs: [],
      personalRecords: [],
      memberGoal: '—',
      memberLevel: '—',
      memberTrainingDays: 0,
    memberScheduledDays: [],
      assignedCoach: null,
      selectedCoachId: null,
      favPrograms: [],
      favProgramIds: [],
      favProgramDetails: [],
      localFavSlugs: [],
      catMuscleFilter: 'todos',
      assignments: [],
      realPrograms: {},
      progressPhotos: [],
      chatOpen: false,
      chatMessages: [],
      chatPartnerId: null,
      chatPartnerName: '',
      unreadMessages: 0,
    });
  }

  async loginWithGoogle() {
    this.setState({ authLoading: true, authError: '' });
    await waitForSupabase();
    // Build the redirect URL ourselves (skipBrowserRedirect) and navigate
    // explicitly — relying on the SDK's internal redirect left the button
    // stuck on "Cargando..." forever if that internal navigation silently
    // didn't happen, which looked like the app "resetting" to the user.
    const { data, error } = await getSupabase().auth.signInWithOAuth({
      provider: 'google',
      options: { redirectTo: window.location.origin + window.location.pathname, skipBrowserRedirect: true },
    });
    if (error) {
      this.setState({ authLoading: false, authError: error.message });
      return;
    }
    if (!data || !data.url) {
      this.setState({ authLoading: false, authError: 'No se pudo iniciar el inicio de sesión con Google. Intenta de nuevo.' });
      return;
    }
    window.location.assign(data.url);
    // Safety net: if the browser is still on this page 4s later, the
    // navigation didn't actually happen — don't leave the button stuck.
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (this.state.authLoading) {
        this.setState({ authLoading: false, authError: 'No se pudo abrir la pantalla de Google. Revisa que tu navegador no esté bloqueando la redirección, e intenta de nuevo.' });
      }
    }, 4000);
  }

  toggleDay(d) {
    this.setState(s => ({
      selectedDays: s.selectedDays.includes(d)
        ? s.selectedDays.filter(x => x !== d)
        : [...s.selectedDays, d],
    }));
  }

  async startWorkoutSession() {
    // Memoriza el programa como "reciente" (solo programas de la colección)
    try {
      const _slug = this.state.selectedProgramId;
      if (_slug && !/^assigned/.test(_slug)) {
        const rec = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.lsKey('vg_recents')) || '[]').filter(s => s !== _slug);
        rec.unshift(_slug);
        localStorage.setItem(this.lsKey('vg_recents'), JSON.stringify(rec.slice(0, 5)));
      }
    } catch (_) {}
    this._workoutStartedAt = Date.now();
    clearInterval(this._timerInterval);
    this._timerInterval = setInterval(() => {
      this.setState({ workoutElapsed: Math.floor((Date.now() - this._workoutStartedAt) / 1000) });
    }, 1000);
    this.setState({
      workoutOpen: false, workoutSessionOpen: true, workoutElapsed: 0, completedEx: [],
      exWeights: {}, logError: '', currentWorkoutLogId: null,
      restSeconds: null,
    });
    if (this.state.session) {
      await waitForSupabase();
      const real = this.state.realPrograms[this.state.selectedProgramId];
      // duration_minutes starts as a placeholder and gets corrected to the
      // real elapsed time in finishWorkoutSession() once we know it.
      const { data, error } = await getSupabase().from('workout_logs')
        .insert({
          member_id: this.state.session.user.id,
          program_id: real ? real.id : null,
          duration_minutes: 1,
        })
        .select('id')
        .single();
      if (!error && data) this.setState({ currentWorkoutLogId: data.id });
    }
  }

  toggleExDone(idx) {
    this.setState(s => {
      const next = s.completedEx.includes(idx)
        ? s.completedEx.filter(i => i !== idx)
        : [...s.completedEx, idx];
      return { completedEx: next };
    });
  }

  setExWeight(idx, value) {
    this.setState(s => ({ exWeights: { ...s.exWeights, [idx]: value } }));
  }

  // Báscula inteligente por Web Bluetooth: busca el servicio estándar de
  // composición corporal (0x181B) o de peso (0x181D) y escucha mediciones.
  async connectSmartScale() {
    if (!navigator.bluetooth) {
      alert('Este navegador no soporta Bluetooth. Abre la app en Chrome (Android) para conectar la báscula. Mientras tanto puedes registrar los datos manualmente tocando cada tarjeta.');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const device = await navigator.bluetooth.requestDevice({
        acceptAllDevices: true,
        optionalServices: ['body_composition', 'weight_scale'],
      });
      const server = await device.gatt.connect();
      let ch = null;
      try {
        const svc = await server.getPrimaryService('body_composition');
        ch = await svc.getCharacteristic('body_composition_measurement');
      } catch (_) {
        const svc = await server.getPrimaryService('weight_scale');
        ch = await svc.getCharacteristic('weight_measurement');
      }
      await ch.startNotifications();
      alert('Báscula "' + (device.name || 'sin nombre') + '" conectada. Súbete a la báscula para registrar tu medición.');
      ch.addEventListener('characteristicvaluechanged', (ev) => {
        try {
          const dv = ev.target.value;
          const flags = dv.getUint16(0, true);
          // Peso: campo estándar en resolución 0.005 kg (BCS) / 0.005 kg (WSS)
          const weightRaw = dv.getUint16(dv.byteLength - 2, true);
          const kg = Math.round(weightRaw * 0.005 * 10) / 10;
          if (kg > 10 && kg < 400) {
            const cur = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('vg_body') || '{}');
            cur.weight = kg;
            cur.weight_at = new Date().toISOString();
            localStorage.setItem('vg_body', JSON.stringify(cur));
            this.syncBodyData(cur);
            this.setState({ bodyDataTick: Date.now() });
          }
        } catch (_) {}
      });
    } catch (err) {
      if (err && err.name === 'NotFoundError') return; // usuario canceló el selector
      alert('No se pudo conectar: ' + (err.message || err) + '. Verifica que la báscula esté encendida y en modo de emparejamiento.');
    }
  }

  // Composición corporal — datos manuales (o de báscula inteligente a futuro)
  editBodyField(key, label, unit) {
    let current = {};
    try { current = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('vg_body') || '{}'); } catch (_) {}
    const val = prompt(label + (current[key] ? ' (actual: ' + current[key] + unit + ')' : ''), current[key] || '');
    if (val === null) return;
    const num = parseFloat(val);
    if (val !== '' && isNaN(num)) { alert('Ingresa un número válido.'); return; }
    current[key] = val === '' ? '' : num;
    current[key + '_at'] = new Date().toISOString();
    try { localStorage.setItem('vg_body', JSON.stringify(current)); } catch (_) {}
    this.syncBodyData(current);
    this.setState({ bodyDataTick: Date.now() });
  }

  syncBodyData(data) {
    // sube la composición corporal a Supabase para que el coach la vea en Progreso
    if (!this.state.session || this.state.userType === 'trainer') return;
    const payload = { profile_id: this.state.session.user.id, body_data: data };
    if (data.weight) payload.weight_kg = data.weight;
    try {
      waitForSupabase().then(() => getSupabase().from('member_profiles').upsert(payload, { onConflict: 'profile_id' })).then(() => {}).catch(() => {});
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  rememberWeight(ex, value) {
    if (!ex || !ex.name || !value) return;
    try {
      const map = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('vg_weights') || '{}');
      map[ex.name] = value;
      localStorage.setItem('vg_weights', JSON.stringify(map));
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  async openCamera() {
    const nextIdx = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].find(i => !this.state.completedEx.includes(i)) ?? 0;
    this.setState({ cameraError: '', recordedVideoUrl: null, recordingExIdx: nextIdx, restSeconds: null });
    try {
      const stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ video: true, audio: false });
      this._cameraStream = stream;
      this.setState({ cameraOpen: true });
      // Video element is plain DOM (not template-bound) so we attach the stream directly once it mounts.
      setTimeout(() => {
        const video = document.getElementById('workout-camera-preview');
        if (video) { video.srcObject = stream; video.play().catch(() => {}); }
      }, 50);
    } catch (err) {
      this.setState({ cameraError: 'No se pudo acceder a la cámara. Revisa los permisos del navegador.' });
    }
  }

  closeCamera() {
    if (this._cameraStream) {
      this._cameraStream.getTracks().forEach(t => t.stop());
      this._cameraStream = null;
    }
    if (this._mediaRecorder && this._mediaRecorder.state !== 'inactive') {
      this._mediaRecorder.stop();
    }
    if (this._restInterval) { clearInterval(this._restInterval); this._restInterval = null; }
    this.setState({ cameraOpen: false, isRecording: false, restSeconds: null });
  }

  toggleRecording() {
    if (!this._cameraStream) return;
    if (this.state.isRecording) {
      this._mediaRecorder.stop();
      this.setState({ isRecording: false });
      return;
    }
    this._recordedChunks = [];
    this._mediaRecorder = new MediaRecorder(this._cameraStream);
    this._mediaRecorder.ondataavailable = (e) => { if (e.data.size > 0) this._recordedChunks.push(e.data); };
    this._mediaRecorder.onstop = () => {
      const blob = new Blob(this._recordedChunks, { type: 'video/webm' });
      this._recordedBlob = blob;
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      this.setState({ recordedVideoUrl: url });
      setTimeout(() => {
        const video = document.getElementById('workout-recorded-video');
        if (video) video.src = url;
      }, 50);
    };
    this._mediaRecorder.start();
    this.setState({ isRecording: true, recordedVideoUrl: null });
  }

  startRest() {
    if (this._restInterval) clearInterval(this._restInterval);
    this.setState({ restSeconds: 60 });
    this._restInterval = setInterval(() => {
      this.setState(s => {
        if (s.restSeconds <= 1) {
          clearInterval(this._restInterval);
          this._restInterval = null;
          return { restSeconds: null };
        }
        return { restSeconds: s.restSeconds - 1 };
      });
    }, 1000);
  }

  async finishExercise() {
    const idx = this.state.recordingExIdx;
    const real = this.state.realPrograms[this.state.selectedProgramId];
    const realEx = real && real.exerciseList ? real.exerciseList[idx] : null;
    const mockNames = ['Press de Banca con Barra', 'Press Inclinado Mancuernas', 'Fondos en Paralelas', 'Press Francés Barra EZ', 'Extensiones Tríceps Polea', 'Flexiones Diamante'];
    const exName = (realEx && realEx.name) || mockNames[idx] || `Ejercicio ${idx + 1}`;
    const weight = this.state.exWeights[idx] || null;

    if (this.state.isRecording && this._mediaRecorder) {
      this._mediaRecorder.stop();
      this.setState({ isRecording: false });
    }

    if (this.state.session && this.state.currentWorkoutLogId) {
      await waitForSupabase();
      const supabaseClient = getSupabase();
      let videoPath = null;
      if (this._recordedBlob) {
        const path = `${this.state.session.user.id}/${this.state.currentWorkoutLogId}-ex${idx}-${Date.now()}.webm`;
        const { error: uploadError } = await supabaseClient.storage
          .from('exercise-videos')
          .upload(path, this._recordedBlob, { contentType: 'video/webm' });
        if (!uploadError) videoPath = path;
        this._recordedBlob = null;
      }
      await supabaseClient.from('exercise_logs').insert({
        workout_log_id: this.state.currentWorkoutLogId,
        member_id: this.state.session.user.id,
        program_exercise_id: realEx ? realEx.id : null,
        exercise_name: exName,
        weight_kg: weight,
        video_path: videoPath,
      });
    }

    this.toggleExDone(idx);
    this.closeCamera();
    const nextIdx = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].find(i => i !== idx && !this.state.completedEx.includes(i) && i !== idx);
    if (nextIdx !== undefined) {
      setTimeout(() => this.openCamera(), 200);
    }
  }

  async finishWorkoutSession() {
    if (this.state.workoutLogging) return;
    clearInterval(this._timerInterval);
    this._timerInterval = null;
    this.closeCamera();
    // Toda sesión terminada cuenta al menos 1 minuto — antes las pruebas
    // cortas redondeaban a 0 y desaparecían de todas las estadísticas.
    const elapsedMinutes = this._workoutStartedAt
      ? Math.max(1, Math.round((Date.now() - this._workoutStartedAt) / 60000))
      : 1;
    // Mapa de pesos por nombre de ejercicio, para que el coach los vea
    let weightNote = '';
    try {
      const _rp = this.state.realPrograms || {};
      const _pid = this.state.selectedProgramId;
      const _prog = _rp[_pid] || _rp['assigned'] || _rp['fuerza'];
      const _exList = (_prog && _prog.exerciseList) || [];
      const _pairs = [];
      Object.keys(this.state.exWeights || {}).forEach(k => {
        const w = this.state.exWeights[k];
        const ex = _exList[k];
        if (w && ex && ex.name) _pairs.push(ex.name + ': ' + w + 'kg');
      });
      if (_pairs.length) weightNote = '__pesos:' + _pairs.join(' · ');
    } catch (_) {}
    if (this.state.session && this.state.currentWorkoutLogId) {
