      await waitForSupabase();
      // Intenta guardar los pesos en notes; si la columna no existe, solo la duración
      let upd = await getSupabase().from('workout_logs')
        .update({ duration_minutes: elapsedMinutes, notes: weightNote })
        .eq('id', this.state.currentWorkoutLogId);
      if (upd.error) {
        await getSupabase().from('workout_logs')
          .update({ duration_minutes: elapsedMinutes })
          .eq('id', this.state.currentWorkoutLogId);
      }
    }
    this._workoutStartedAt = null;
    this.setState({ workoutLogging: false, workoutSessionOpen: false, workoutJustLogged: true });
    setTimeout(() => this.setState({ workoutJustLogged: false }), 3000);
    this.fetchStats();
  }

  async finishOnboarding() {
    const goalMap = { fuerza: 'muscle', peso: 'fat_loss', salud: 'health', rendimiento: 'performance' };
    const levelMap = { principiante: 'beginner', intermedio: 'intermediate', avanzado: 'advanced' };
    this.setState(s => ({ onboardingStep: 8, screen: s.userType === 'trainer' ? 'coach' : 'home' }));
    if (!this.state.session) {
      // No real Supabase session yet (e.g. email confirmation/rate limit
      // pending) — nothing to save to. Make this visible instead of silently
      // dropping the user's goal/level/days on the floor.
      console.warn('[onboarding] no session — goal/level/days were not saved to member_profiles');
      alert('No se pudo guardar tu objetivo/nivel/días porque tu sesión no quedó confirmada (revisa tu correo o vuelve a iniciar sesión). Puedes editarlo después desde Perfil.');
      return;
    }
    if (this.state.userType !== 'trainer') {
      await waitForSupabase();
      const { error } = await getSupabase().from('member_profiles').upsert({
        profile_id: this.state.session.user.id,
        goal: goalMap[this.state.selectedGoal] || null,
        level: levelMap[this.state.selectedLevel] || null,
        training_days: this.state.selectedDays,
        preferred_hours: this.state.preferredHours,
        weight_kg: this.state.weightKg ? parseFloat(this.state.weightKg) : null,
        height_cm: this.state.heightCm ? parseFloat(this.state.heightCm) : null,
      }, { onConflict: 'profile_id' });
      if (error) {
        console.error('[onboarding] member_profiles upsert failed:', error);
        alert('No se pudo guardar tu perfil: ' + error.message);
        return;
      }
      this.fetchMemberProfile();
      this.fetchPrograms();
    }
  }

  async confirmCoachPayment() {
    const list = this.state.coaches || [];
    const coach = list.find(c => c.id === this.state.selectedCoachId);
    if (!coach) return;
    this.setState({ onboardingStep: 7 });
    if (coach.real && this.state.session) {
      this.sendPosRequest('coach', coach.id, coach.name, parseFloat(String(coach.price || '').replace(/[^0-9.]/g, '')) || null);
      alert('Solicitud enviada. Tu entrenador queda pendiente de pago — pásalo a pagar en recepción y quedará activo.');
    }
  }

  async sendPosRequest(type, refId, refName, price) {
    // la solicitud aparece en el inicio del POS para cobrarse en recepción
    if (!this.state.session) return;
    try {
      await waitForSupabase();
      await getSupabase().from('pos_requests').insert({
        member_id: this.state.session.user.id, type: type, ref_id: refId || null,
        ref_name: refName || null, price: price || null,
        branch_id: this.state.memberBranchId || null,
      });
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  async fetchPlansCatalog() {
    try {
      await waitForSupabase();
      let res = await getSupabase().from('plans').select('id, name, price, duration_days, is_family, branch_id, active').eq('active', true).order('duration_days');
      if (res.error) res = await getSupabase().from('plans').select('id, name, price, duration_days, is_family, active').eq('active', true).order('duration_days');
      const data = res.data || [];
      const b = this.state.memberBranchId;
      this.setState({ plansCatalog: data.filter(p => !p.branch_id || p.branch_id === b) });
    } catch (_) {}
  }

  async requestPlan(p) {
    if (this._reqBusy) return;
    this._reqBusy = true;
    try {
      await waitForSupabase();
      const { data: dup } = await getSupabase().from('pos_requests')
        .select('id').eq('member_id', this.state.session.user.id).eq('type', 'plan').eq('status', 'pendiente').limit(1);
      if (dup && dup.length) {
        this.setState({ planReqSent: 'Ya tienes una solicitud pendiente. Pásala a pagar en recepción antes de pedir otra.' });
        return;
      }
      await this.sendPosRequest('plan', p.id, p.name, p.price);
      this.setState({ planReqSent: 'Solicitud enviada: ' + p.name + '. Pásala a pagar en recepción y tu membresía queda activa.', planReqOpen: false });
      alert('Solicitud de ' + p.name + ' enviada. Pasa a recepción a pagarla.');
    } finally { this._reqBusy = false; }
  }

  toggleFav(id) {
    this.setState(s => ({
      favPrograms: s.favPrograms.includes(id)
        ? s.favPrograms.filter(x => x !== id)
        : [...s.favPrograms, id],
    }));
  }

  renderVals() {
    if (!this._pwaDone) {
      this._pwaDone = true;
      try {
        document.title = 'Volten Gym';
        var _h = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        if (_h && !document.querySelector('link[rel=manifest]')) {
          var _t = [['link', { rel: 'manifest', href: 'manifest.json' }], ['link', { rel: 'icon', type: 'image/png', href: 'voltengym.png' }], ['link', { rel: 'apple-touch-icon', href: 'voltengym.png' }], ['meta', { name: 'theme-color', content: '#F97316' }]];
          for (var _i = 0; _i < _t.length; _i++) {
            var _e = document.createElement(_t[_i][0]);
            for (var _k in _t[_i][1]) _e.setAttribute(_k, _t[_i][1][_k]);
            _h.appendChild(_e);
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {}
    }
    const { onboardingStep, screen, workoutOpen, selectedGoal, selectedLevel, selectedDays, userName, userEmail, activeFilter, showNotifications, favPrograms, authMode, userType, selectedProgramId, authError, authLoading, selectedCoachId, assignedCoach, coaches, workoutLogging } = this.state;
    const rawCoachList = coaches || [];
    const hoursMatch = (preferred, coachHours) => {
      if (!preferred || preferred === 'flexible') return 'match';
      if (!coachHours) return 'unknown';
      const h = coachHours.toLowerCase();
      // Detect specific time ranges in the hours string
      const hasEveningPm = /[4-9]pm|10pm|noche/.test(h);
      const hasAfternoonPm = /12pm|1pm|2pm|3pm|4pm|tarde/.test(h);
      const hasMorningAm = /[5-9]am|10am|11am|mañana/.test(h);
      const hasOnlyMorning = hasMorningAm && !hasAfternoonPm && !hasEveningPm;
      if (preferred === 'morning') return (hasMorningAm) ? 'match' : 'other';
      if (preferred === 'evening') return hasEveningPm ? 'match' : 'other';
      if (preferred === 'afternoon') return (hasAfternoonPm && !hasOnlyMorning) ? 'match' : 'other';
      return 'unknown';
    };
    const sortOrder = { match: 0, unknown: 1, other: 2 };
    const coachList = [...rawCoachList].sort((a, b) =>
      (sortOrder[hoursMatch(this.state.preferredHours, a.hours)] ?? 1) -
      (sortOrder[hoursMatch(this.state.preferredHours, b.hours)] ?? 1)
    );
    const pickedCoach = selectedCoachId ? coachList.find(c => c.id === selectedCoachId) : null;
    const isOnb = onboardingStep < 8;

    // Workout data by program — uses real exercise_catalog data when loaded.
    const _ce = this.state.curatedExercises || {};
    const _exFor = (cat, fallbackNames) => {
      const real = _ce[cat];
      if (real && real.length) return real;
      return fallbackNames.map(n => ({ name: n, subtitle: '', setsReps: '3 × 12' }));
    };
    const progData = {
      fuerza:    { name: 'Fuerza Total',    subtitle: 'Fuerza Total · Activo',     category: 'FUERZA',    duration: '45', level: 'Intermedio',  exercises: '5', exerciseList: [{ name: 'Press de Banca', subtitle: 'Pecho', setsReps: '4 × 8' }, { name: 'Sentadilla', subtitle: 'Pierna', setsReps: '4 × 10' }, { name: 'Peso Muerto', subtitle: 'Espalda baja', setsReps: '4 × 6' }, { name: 'Dominadas', subtitle: 'Espalda', setsReps: '3 × 8' }, { name: 'Press Militar', subtitle: 'Hombro', setsReps: '3 × 10' }] },
      hiit:      { name: 'HIIT Explosivo',  subtitle: 'HIIT Explosivo · Activo',   category: 'HIIT',      duration: '30', level: 'Avanzado',    exercises: String(_exFor('cardio',['Sprints','Jumping Jacks','Bicicleta','Elíptica']).length), exerciseList: _exFor('cardio',['Sprints','Jumping Jacks','Bicicleta','Elíptica']) },
      movilidad: { name: 'Movilidad Pro',   subtitle: 'Movilidad Pro · Activo',    category: 'MOVILIDAD', duration: '40', level: 'Principiante', exercises: String(_exFor('movilidad',['Rotaciones Cadera','Cat-Cow','Estiramiento Isquios']).length), exerciseList: _exFor('movilidad',['Rotaciones Cadera','Cat-Cow','Estiramiento Isquios']) },
      cardio:    { name: 'Cardio Base',     subtitle: 'Cardio Base · Activo',      category: 'CARDIO',    duration: '35', level: 'Principiante', exercises: '4', exerciseList: [{ name: 'Caminadora', subtitle: 'Calentamiento + ritmo', setsReps: '15 min' }, { name: 'Bicicleta Estática', subtitle: 'Ritmo moderado', setsReps: '10 min' }, { name: 'Elíptica', subtitle: 'Resistencia media', setsReps: '8 min' }, { name: 'Saltar Cuerda', subtitle: 'Para cerrar', setsReps: '3 × 1 min' }] },
      espalda:   { name: 'Fuerza y Espalda',subtitle: 'Fuerza y Espalda · Activo', category: 'FUERZA',    duration: '45', level: 'Intermedio',  exercises: '6', exerciseList: [{ name: 'Remo con Barra', subtitle: 'Espalda media', setsReps: '4 × 10' }, { name: 'Dominadas', subtitle: 'Dorsal ancho', setsReps: '3 × 8' }, { name: 'Jalón al Pecho', subtitle: 'Polea alta', setsReps: '3 × 12' }, { name: 'Remo en Máquina', subtitle: 'Espalda media', setsReps: '3 × 12' }, { name: 'Peso Muerto', subtitle: 'Cadena posterior', setsReps: '4 × 6' }, { name: 'Hiperextensiones', subtitle: 'Espalda baja', setsReps: '3 × 15' }] },

        acc[`log${i}Program`] = progName;

        acc[`log${i}Duration`] = log ? log.duration : '';
        return acc;

          // Generación local (funciona sin depender de servicios de imágenes).
          if (window.qrcode) {
            try {
              const qr = window.qrcode(0, 'M');
              qr.addData(payload);
              qr.make();
              img.src = qr.createDataURL(8, 12);
              return;
            } catch (_) {}
          }
          // Respaldo si la librería no cargó
          img.src = 'https://api.qrserver.com/v1/create-qr-code/?size=200x200&margin=10&data=' + encodeURIComponent(payload);
